                                                                                                        """
                                                                                                        This function calculates the Michelin rating for a given metal.
                                                                                                    
                                                                                                        Args:
                                                                                                            a: A string representing the metal's properties (e.g., "aluminum", "steel").
                                                                                                    
                                                                                                        Returns:
                                                                                                            A string containing the Michelin rating.
                                                                                                        """
                                                                                                        if a == "aluminum":
                                                                                                            return "Good"
                                                                                                        elif a == "steel":
                                                                                                            return "Excellent"
                                                                                                        elif a == "copper":
                                                                                                            return "Good"
                                                                                                        elif a == "nickel":
                                                                                                            return "Excellent"
                                                                                                        elif a == "gold":
                                                                                                            return "Excellent"
                                                                                                        elif a == "platinum":
                                                                                                            return "Excellent"
                                                                                                        else:
                                                                                                            return "Poor"
                                                                                                    
                                                                                                    # Example usage:
                                                                                                    print(Michelin_manifeste("aluminum")) # Output: Good
                                                                                                    print(Michelin_manifeste("steel")) # Output: Excellent
                                                                                                    print(Michelin_manifeste("copper")) # Output: Good
                                                                                                    print(Michelin_manifeste("nickel")) # Output: Excellent
                                                                                                    print(Michelin_manifeste("gold")) # Output: Excellent
                                                                                                    print(Michelin_manifeste("platinum")) # Output: Excellent
                                                                                                    ```
